    private void OnDisable()
    {
        EventMgr.UnregisterEvent(gameObject);
    }

    EvolutionData mData = null;

    public override void InitData(object data)
    {
        mData = data as EvolutionData;

        RefreshData();
    }

    private void RefreshData()
    {
        if (mData != null && mData.ConfigData!=null)
        {
            gameObject.name=mData.ConfigData.SoldierType.ToString();
            var rdyToUnlock = mData.ReadyToEvolute;
            var nextMeta = mData.GetNextMeta();

            rightGo.SetActive(nextMeta!=null);
            lockGo.SetActive(nextMeta == null);

            btn_evo.SetActive(rdyToUnlock);
            btn_updrade.SetActive(!rdyToUnlock && mData.CanToUp);
            if(btn_next != null)
            {
                btn_next.SetActive(nextMeta != null);
            }

            UIHelper.SetImage(lefticon
